msg:The weather was not very good this time. It was cloudy and it rained at night. The morning after the rain was different, misty and like a landscape painting.
The lake water was a little black and had a strange smell, which affected the walk by the lake.
The room was fully equipped. I liked the furniture on the balcony, which I didn't know whether to call a sofa or a chair. It was big enough to sleep on it. I lay down and felt the spring breeze, especially in the early morning after the rain. The air was very good. People were very relaxed at that time.
The hotel is in the mountains and there are no other buildings around, so it is very quiet. It is so quiet that you can hear the voices of people walking by the lake on the 9th floor.
Many entertainment projects are not open in this season, and basically there is only a place to exercise on the 2nd floor. There are gyms, table tennis rooms, billiard rooms, etc., and an indoor swimming pool (the outdoor one is not open yet). I went to the swimming pool for a while in the evening, and there were not many people. There are toilets, showers, changing rooms, etc. in the swimming pool area, but you need to bring your own swimsuit and swimming cap. You can also buy them at the service desk.
The breakfast is also very rich, and it is even open until 10:30 on Sundays.
I plan to take a short vacation after the water activities open in the summer. It should be more fun then.

name:C‚Äçe‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçc‚Äçh‚Äçe‚Äçn
info:1 King Premium Lake View  Balcony
info:Stayed in January 2023
info:Family
info:8 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted January 30, 2023
msg:The hotel is a distance from Qiandao Lake, more than an hour's drive, and closer to Jiande Railway Station. There is a pick-up station every day during the Spring Festival.
advantage:
1. The room is large. The balcony and bathroom of the deluxe lake view double room we booked are very large, and there is also a dressing room. The balcony looks very nice! Take a bath while watching fireworks at night.
2. There are quite a lot of items in the entertainment center of the hotel. I played kayaking. Although it is very cold in winter, it is sunny and fun. The wharf management staff saw that our family of three father was too heavy to paddle, so they changed boats on the water halfway, and provided a separate boat for my father. The service attitude is awesome!
3. Jingmei. The view in front of the hotel is really amazing! Much more beautiful than Qiandao Lake Central Lake Scenic Area! You can also see the Xin'an River Dam.
4. The free fish head voucher can be used as a set meal in the Chinese restaurant, and the fish head soup tastes good.
5. Because the hotel is in Jiande, you can also play Daci Rock and Lingxi Cave. Both places are 4A. We all think it is more fun than Qiandao Lake! If you have time, you must go to Daciyan! ! !
6. The air conditioner in the room is powerful! The first day I entered the room, I was so hot that I was sweating. It was closed in the middle of the night, and it was still very hot inside with zero degrees outside. There is no such thing as poor air conditioning in the room as mentioned in other reviews.
7. During the Spring Festival, you can go to the Southeast Lake Scenic Area by the pier next to the hotel! There is no need to drive for more than an hour, and the scenery of Southeast Lake is better than that of Central Lake, which is very commercial!
shortcoming:
1. The traffic is inconvenient. We have taken a taxi during the Spring Festival this time, but if we go to Daciyan and Lingxi Cave for a day, it is recommended to charter a car or drive by ourselves. It is said that there are many mountain roads in Jiande, and it is also cost-effective to charter a car if you are not used to mountain roads. On the last day I went to the train station and couldn't get a taxi. Fortunately, the taxi left a phone call to pick it up the day before, otherwise I would not be able to catch the train. So don't even think about taking a taxi.
2. The bathroom has no ventilation and no windows, so it has a peculiar smell. Therefore, we open the balcony door every day when we go out, but it seems that there are no screen doors on the balcony where there are many mosquitoes in summer.
3. Hot water: One day my husband took a bath and said that the water was lukewarm but not hot at all. Probably too many people. I did not find this problem.
4. The breakfast is not rich, but it can be full. There are Jiande tofu buns. There are not many things in the evening buffet.
5. What I want to say most is hygiene, it's a bit rough! The room is big, but not well cleaned. There are cotton swabs on the floor next to the bedside table, dust on the table around the side, and hair from breakfast.

Generally speaking, it is quite good to live here and play Jiande. If there is no boat on the nearby pier in Southeast Lake during non-holidays, it is not worthwhile. It is too far from the two piers of Qiandao Lake. Because of Daciyan, I am very satisfied!

It is hidden in the green mountains and green waters. The modern design is like a cruise ship sailing. 2. The hotel has well-equipped facilities and is suitable for parent-child play. There is an information center booth in the lobby, where all play items are displayed. Children can feed fish at the door. The hotel also has other parent-child play items, karting, bumper cars, family bicycles, There are also Mavericks battery car, archery trampoline and so on. 3. If the distance is long and it is inconvenient to drive, the hotel also has new energy vehicles that can be rented in the case of high oil prices, which can be accompanied by a driver or self-driving. 4. The hotel has 3 swimming pools, one indoor and one outdoor on the 2nd floor. The indoor is a constant temperature swimming pool, but I still prefer the outdoor infinity pool, which is clean and produced on the cruise plywood; there is another one on the 1st floor facing the lake, Looking at all the star-rated hotels in Qiandao Lake, I can't find a swimming pool that is closer to the lake than this. 5. There is also a pier in front of the hotel. In the evening, many people are playing motorboats and other water sports. 6. The hotel not only has complete facilities but also very good service. From the front desk to the guest room to the restaurant staff are very friendly, and the front desk will take the initiative to send a souvenir when checking out.
7. Tips: If you stay in this hotel in July and August, it is recommended that you stagger the time between 2 and 3 o'clock. There are many Nongfu Spring factories next to the hotel and many large trucks will be encountered.
All in all, it was a very pleasant holiday, and I will definitely come again next time!
